msg:I originally booked a deluxe twin room by the river, but it rained heavily these days and the sound of water was deafening, so I changed to a loft twin room. In fact, I usually like this double-story room type. The ceiling is too low and a bit depressing, but it is more convenient for a family of three to sleep. The loft big bed opens to the square, which is more convenient for going out.

The surrounding environment is superb, surrounded by mountains on three sides, the water vapor is pleasing to the eyes, and the Yadong River is wide and open. It would be great if you can go down to play. There is a large lawn behind, and there is a market, and behind it is a design exhibition. You can walk the dog, fly kites, and have a picnic on the lawn.

The hotel restaurant is the most added part. I had a group-purchased dinner and breakfast. Every dish was very delicious. There were also seasonal mugwort rice rolls and cakes. The restaurant environment was wide and transparent. It felt especially good to have breakfast early in the morning while looking at the green mountains and green waters.

The housekeeper Xiaokang was very helpful, responded very promptly, and knew all the details of the room. When there was no hot water for the shower, he opened another room in time to take a shower, and sent additional water and lychee tea.

The room facilities are reasonably designed. There is also a toilet on the second floor. The lighting control is very clear. The hot spring is large and clean. There is also a ginseng fruit tree in the yard.

The place for improvement is that the birthday decoration is too simple. There is only a towel cake, which is better than nothing. There is no sense of ceremony at all. I specifically look for a place to celebrate my birthday.

name:S‚Äçh‚Äçu‚Äçs‚Äçe
info:Loft Villa
info:Stayed in March 2022
info:Other
info:84 Reviews
rating:4
posted:Posted March 25, 2022
msg:Customers come to consume, not to be kidnapped to write 5-point praise!
The essential difference between consumption and service is completely ignored:
As a consumer, paying for hotel services and enjoying them is a matter of course! Its check-in experience and evaluation are objective feelings about the match between price and service! However, post-consumer is required to complete assignments and write reviews within a time limit. This is really absurd, and it is the original inversion of the relationship between business and consumption!
Adding a housekeeper, euphemistically, is to facilitate customers to enjoy attentive service during their stay, and its real purpose is to brush up on praise! Butlers would play the pitiful role of asking customers to write five-star reviews so they wouldn't be deducted from their bonuses. At the same time, customers will be required to make it within 24 hours of leaving the store, with a maximum of 48 hours!
Writing a review is no longer voluntary by customers, but completed within a limited time by various emotions. What logic is this? Customers come to consume, not to complete work. Has the store owner considered this essential issue? What's more, this kind of situation abounds in domestic hotels, and we have to think, why is this deformed hotel chaos flourishing?
Back to my review of this hotel. In general, the surrounding environment of the hotel is very good, the architectural style is very novel, and the hardware and software equipment is new. The overall service level of the staff is relatively professional. From the hotel security, to the front desk, cleaners, restaurant waiters and other hotel staff, the service level in the Conghua area has reached the first-class level.
In particular, the catering is also the most outstanding part of this hotel. The lunch and dinner are good, and there are various special packages for two to six people, which can kill a lot of surrounding farmhouses! Considering the three aspects of ingredients, cooking skills and price, it is first-class in the Conghua hot spring area. It is also a training base for chefs, and the cooking skills are quite good! What's more worth mentioning, the buffet breakfast provides many classic Cantonese morning tea and dim sum for the hotel's characteristics of local tourists. This time I came here, and I especially liked his newly added beef lasagna, pork trotters, ginger vinegar eggs, and various raw porridge, which are a must-eat every time you come. They are also popular Cantonese classics! The only thing that needs to be improved is that wonton is a very good classic food in Guangdong. The products here are slightly inferior, the skin is thick and the filling is not fresh enough. If it can be improved, it will be even better! It can be said objectively that the production and positioning of this hotel's buffet breakfast is absolutely outstanding compared to several five-star hot spring hotels surrounding it.

The new hotel room has a faint aroma. The butler Xiao Wu and Xiaodan are attentive and thoughtful throughout the process. They have prepared fruit plates and dried fruits. The Yazui River at the door is great. I took two bales to fish for an afternoon. After the meal, you can ride along the side of the hotel to ride a bike, fly a kite, have a picnic, run and take a walk, which is particularly comfortable. The framing is good. When the weather gets cold later, I will meet up with friends again.
